 philhal 13000 squaire feet main faile hare ped paudhon se las is tarah kaa ek oxigen chembar huda city centre metro stesan par taiyaar he
 Where people can feel the pure air of this chamber

 manochikitsakon ne is baat kii jaankaree di

 Mr

 " Cinnamon, one of the main spices present in the kitchen, is used for flavors
 haalanki kam hi logon ko yah jaankaree he ki yah dil ke liye bahut hi phydemand he
 Consumption of cinnamon provides relief in many heart related problems
 darasal, isamen fibre or calcium acchhee maatra main paae jate hai or inaki madad sebed cholestrol kaa str kam hota he
 The decrease of such cholesterol reduces the risk of arterial blockage
 jaaniye dalacheenee ke or phaayde:1
 For relief in winter, if you have a cold, then cinnamon intake will be beneficial for you
 shahad ke saath dalacheenee kaa powder subah-shaam lene se phayda hoga
 If you have a headache due to cold, then its application will benefit
 2
 Cinnamon is extremely beneficial for joint pain
 halke garm pani main dalacheenee or shahad milakar pine se aaraam miltaa he
 Massaging with its oil also proves beneficial
 3
 Making heart and cinnamon powder paste for heart patients does not accumulate cholesterol in the arteries and reduces the risk of heart attack
 jin logon ko pehle bhi heart atake aa chukaa he, unhen is upaay ko karne se phayda milegaa or dobaaraa atake padane kii ashanka bhi kam ho jaaegi
 4
 cholestrol kam karne ke liedgar aapkaa cholestrol badha hua he or aap use kam karne ke liye prayaas kar rahe hai to dalacheenee kaa istemaal aapke liye phydemand rahegaa
 5
 pet kii samasya ke liedgar aapako apach kii samasya he to dalacheenee kaa istemaal kaa aapke liye phydemand rahegaa
 Apart from this, its use is also beneficial in vomiting and diarrhea
 europe main hue ek shodh ke mutabik jo bachche kaccha doodh pite hai, unhen asthma or allergy kaa khatra ublaa doodh pine vaale bacchonke mukaable kam hota he
 Although this research cannot be considered a very big scientific fact
 shodh se praapt jaankaree ke mutabik doodh ubaalane ke dauraan sharir kii pratirohak kshamta badhaane vaale protein bhi nasht ho jate he

 sabhi saajon kii sangat ke saath samaaj ke swaroop kaa anumaan to isse hi lagata he ki samooh samaaj gayan kii aawaaj bina kisi laudspikar aadi kii sahaayta ke milon dur tak suni ja sakati he
 ' is puri parampara main shringaar aarti evam raatri ko sandhya aarti kaa vishesh mahatv hota he
 Devotees who are drenched by flying gulal consider themselves blessed
 holashtakon se dol panchami tak rang kii prakriya hoti he, ise shabdon se varnan nahin kiya ja saktaa, keval dekhakar hi ise mahasoos kiya ja saktaa he
 Local journalist Sunil Sharma told, 'the special festival starts with the full moon day of Holi
 devalayas main rang gulaal abir choba chandan kii bauchhaarein darshak ke man ko moh leti he
 Holi is worshiped in the evening with the Ordnance plow-pestle, symbol of Shri Thakur ji, which includes thousands of women, children and old people
 yah juluus apni apane tarah kaa sampoorn brij mandal main akelaa hi he
 From the Parikrama road to the Holi worship place, it is about two km, the entire route freezes the base of Gulal Bhubhwar
 shri narayanashram se prarambh yah yatra do ghante main puri hoti hai raatri main ‘bhaagin payo ri sajani yah hori sautyohaar’ kii shabdaawalee antahkaran ko chhu jaati he
 ' pratipada ko mandir main vahi rang-gulaal or dopaher ko saikadon 'bhabhi-devar' mandir ke praangan main paramparaagat maharas kaa aayojan karte hai
 Total Badhus of Sevayatas dance with their dears in distinctive costumes
 shehanai or nagade kii swar-lahari darshakon ke liye divyanubhuti kaa kaaran banati he or darshak us rang main duubakar swayan ko dhanya anubhav karata he
 The Huranga is held on Dwitiya (on 28 March this year)
 praatah 11 baje se hi mandir praangan main rang kii bharmaar ho jaati he
 The traditional color of Tesu is scattered in big hoses
 mandir praangan main tathaa chaaron ore chhaton par darshakon kii bheed main til rakhane kii jagah bhi nahin bachati va sthaneey darshak or videshi paryatak is utsav main barabas khinche chale aate he
 Rajbhog is organized at 12 noon and two flags symbolizing the two brothers are present in the middle of the temple on the orders of Shri Thakur Ji
 idhar, sevaayat goswami varg kii badhuen evam gwaal-bal swaroop pandagan mandir main ekatrit hote hai
 The first dance takes place, after which the game of huranga starts according to Thakur ji's order
 yahaan atyant maryaadit tareeke se hi khel hota he
 Hurriyara men put full colors on their sisters in kunds and hoses and in return the sisters grab their body clothes
 unke upar dandon se prahaar karti hai
 The pure gulas of different colors flying from the rooftops give the ultimate divine feeling to the tune of nagade shehnai below and 'aajri re rasiya in Virj today
 
 
 ' tathaa ‘chhora tote hori jal kheluun, meri pahaunchi main ghungroo jadaay
 
 
 The sound of 'enchants the listener
 tippaniyan The mixture of colors of roses flying in the sky is enchanting
 is varna sammishran hetu anek kalavid yahaan varna sangyojan kaa hi anubhav evam anand lene aate hai
 This huranga game continues till 3 pm
 khel ke madhya virajit jhundon kaa shri revati ji evam shri radha ji ke ishaare par huriyaari lut leti hai or is prakaar utsav purnataa kii ore agrasar hota he tathaa sabhi khiladi parikrama hetu agrasar hote hai tathaa puri parikrama main goonjata he ‘haari re gori ghar chalin auraten, to marungi jehar vish khaay
 
 ’ aadi-aadi
 In this festival, many types of cannabis, especially of cannabis, are kept in the enjoyment of Thakur Ji
 dhyaan rahe, is utsav main 20 man gulaal udata he, jo ki ek ricard he
 Holi is the culmination of Holi on Panchami
 mandir main madhyanh main samaaj rang gulaal hota he tathaa us samaaj kaa bahut ji bhavotpadak par jab gaaya jaataa he to barabas shrota bhav vibhor hokar ashrupat karte dekhe ja sakate hai
 'whoever is playing, he should play jagari with his feet
 
 
 ’ rangon ko ek varsh ke liye vidaai di jaati he
 The director of the Shri Haladhar Holistic Philosophy Research Institute based at Baldev, Dr
 ghanashyam pandeya bataate hai, 'shri daujee mandir main yah utsav magh shukla basant panchami se shuru hokar caitra krishna panchami yani dolotsav tak chalata he
 The traditional folk singing of the temple starts echoing and 'khelat Basant Balabhadra Dev'

 Shringar Aarti and Sandhya Aarti at night have special significance in this tradition
 gulaal udne se sarabor hue shrriddhalu bhakt apane aapako dhanya maanate hai
 There is a color process from Holashtakas to Dole Panchami, it cannot be described with words, it can be felt only by seeing
 sthaneey patrkaar sunil sharma ne bataaya, 'holi kii poornima se vishesh utsav prarambh ho jaataa he
 The shower of Rang Gulal Abir Choba Chandan in the temple captivates the viewer's mind
 shaam ke samay shri thakur ji ke pratik aayudh hal-moosal ke saath holi pujan hota he jisamen hajaaron kii sankhya main mahilaayein bal, vruddh log sammilit hote hai
 This procession is the only one of its kind in the entire Brij Mandal
 parikrama maarg se lekar holi pujan sthal kareeb do kimi he, saare maarg main gulaal bhudbhud kii tahen jam jaati hai
 Starting from Sri Narayanashram, this journey is completed in two hours
 At night, the vocabulary of 'bhagin Paayo Ri Sajni Ye Hori Sautayohar' touches the conscience
 ' Pratipada holds the same color and color in the temple and in the afternoon hundreds of 'bhabhi-dewar' organize traditional Maharas in the temple premises
 sevayaton kii kul badhuen apane devron ke saath vishisht paridhaanon se nrity karti hai
 The sound of shehnai and nagade causes divination for the audience and the viewer feels blessed by being immersed in that color
 dwitiya ke din (is saal 28 march ko) huranga kaa aayojan hota he
 There is a glut of color in the temple premises from 11 am itself
 badi-badi haujon main tesu ke paramparaagat rang kii chata bikhar jaati he
 There is no place to keep mole in the crowd of visitors in the temple courtyard and on the terraces all around, and the local visitors and foreign tourists are drawn to this festival
 dopaher 12 baje rajbhog kaa aayojan hota he tathaa donon bhaaiyon ke pratik do jhande shri thakur ji kii ajna se mandir ke madhya main upasthit hote hai
 Here, the sadhus and gwal-bal Swaroop of Sevayat Goswami class gather in the Pandagan temple
 pehle nrity hota he, uske baad thakur ji kii aagyaanusaar khel huranga prarambh ho jaataa he
 Here the game is played in a very decent manner
 huriyaare purush apni bhabhiyon par kund or haujon main bhare rang daalate jate hai or badale main bhabhiyaan unke sharir ke vastron ko pakadakar khinch leti hai
 Strikes them with sticks
 chhaton se udate hue vibhinn rangon ke shuddh gulaal neeche nagade shehanai kii dhun param divya bhav upasthit kar dete hai or 'aaj viraj main hori re rasiyaa
 
 
 'and' Chhora Parrot should play hori water, it is rooted in my reach
 
 
 ’ kii dhwani shrotaaon ko mugdh kar detii hai

 For this varna blending, many artists come here to experience and enjoy the same combination of varna
 yah huranga kaa khel madhyaantar teen baje tak chalata rahata he
 At the behest of Shri Revati ji and Shri Radha ji of the flaming flocks in the middle of the game, Hurriyari loots and thus the festival moves towards perfection and all the players are marching to the circumambulation and the whole reverberation revolves' Hari re gori ghar chali Women will die if they eat poison
 
 ' etc etc
 is utsav main vishesh kar bhaang ke anekon prakaar ke mishran thakur ji ke bhoga main rakhe jate hai
 Keep in mind, 20 Mana Gulal flies in this festival, which is a record
 panchami ke din holi kii charam pariniti hoti he

 uttar pradesh main congress netaa sonia or rahul gandhi ke khilaaf samaajawaadee party apana ummidavaar khadaa nahin karegi
 This is to say of the Chief Minister of the state Akhilesh Yadav
 akhilesh yadav ne sonia gandhi or rahul gandhi ke sansadeey kshetron raibareli or amethi main pratyaashee khadey karne ke babaat puche gaye sawaal ke jawaab main kaha ki party ke rashtriya adhyaksh mulaayam singh yadav ne abhi tak to koi pratyaashee tay nahin kiya he or isaki sambhaavna bhi nahin he

 India had been waiting for decades for the official data of its people, ie an income data, which is mandatory for every economic decision
 yahaan saamaajik-aarthik surveykshan ke paanch bade nateezon ko jaananaa jaruri he jo nitiyon or siyasat ko prabhavit karengeh (1) bharat main das main saat log gaanv main rahete hai, (2) 30 fisadi log kheti par nirbhar hai or 51 fisadi log sirf majdoor hai, (3) gaanvon main har paanch main chaar pariwaron main sarvaadhik kamaane vaale sadsy kii adhiktam aay 5,000 ru
 Per month
 yani paanch sadasyon ke parivaar main prati vyakti aay prati maah ek hajaar ru
 (4) 56 percent of the rural people are landless, (5) 36 percent are rural illiterate
 keval teen fisadi log graduate hai
 (see 'how India fell behind in this issue')
 These figures only show the economic condition of the rural population
 isi surveykshan kaa shahari hissaa abhi jari hona he
 Which may suggest that 35 million families out of the 11 crore families in the cities have no means of income
 gramin or shahari (anadhikarik) aarthik surveykshan ke teen bade nishkarsh hai
 First, 70 percent of the country's population is rural
 doosraa, shaharon-gaanvon ko milakar kareeb 90 fisadi aabaadi aisi he jo keval 200 se 250 ru
 Per day, and the third is the middle class in India of only 11 crore people who have a safe regular income
 is aankade ke baad koi bhi yah maanegaa ki desh main nitiyon ke gathan kii buniyaad badalane kaa vakt aa gaya he jisaki shuruyaat un paimaanon ko badalane se hogi jo sabhi aarthik-saamaajik nitiyon kaa aadhaar hai
 Without changing the measurement of poverty in the country, it will not work anymore because these figures have proved that poverty in India is more than all previous calculations
 khapat surveykshan, mahangaai kii gananaa, rojgaron kaa hisaab-kitaab, saamaajik suraksha kii jarurat hai
 The formulas will also be decided afresh
 khapat ko aadhaar banaakar bharat main asamanta ghatane kaa jo akalan (ginni koifishient) kiya jaataa rahaa he, is aankade kii roshni main vah bhi badal jayega
 Government policies will appear at a decisive departure point as these parameters change
 saamaajik-aarthik sensos ke aankade sabit karte hai ki bharat main manaregaa jaise kaarykram rajnatik safalataa kyon laate hai? saste anaaj ke sahare raman singh, naveen patnayak yaa saste bhojan ke sahare jayalalita lokapriy or safal kaise bane rahete hai jabaki audyogic nivesh or buniyadi dhaanche kii safalataa par voter nahin rijhate
 However, the statistics also show that the framework of populist policies can only keep people alive, they cannot improve their lives
 arthvyavastha par aarthik sudhaaron ke prabhaav ke samanaantar in aankadon kii gahari padtaal kii jaae to shaayad nitiyon ke ek nae raste kii jarurat mahasoos hogi, jo vikaas ke puure aayojan ko badalane, gavarnence ke bade sudhaar, takneekon kaa istemaal, santulit rup se khule bazaar or nae kism kii skiimon se gadha jayega
 The politics of poverty is certainly bad, but when 90 per cent of the people do not have income security, then there is no work without employment or food-giving schemes
 aise main saamaajik suraksha dene ke nae tareeke khojane honge or rojgaron ko mausami va asthaayee staron se nikaalkar sthaayee kii taraf le janaa hoga
 You can waste your time bashing the Congress over the past six decades of rural plight, but the truth is that this is the right time to come out with these figures
 congress ke raaj main agar ye aankade aae hote to loklubhaavanavaad kaa charam dikh jaataa
 There is now a government at the center which is not bound to bear the burden of the past
 iske paas mauka he ki vah bharat main nitiyon kaa rasayan nae sire se taiyaar kare
 Socio-economic surveys and old experiences suggest that the country does not need a huge maze of policies and schemes
 achook takanic, monitering, rajyon ke saath samanvay se las or teen chaar bade saamaajik kaarykram paryaapt hai, jinhen khule or santulit bazaar ke samanaantar chalaakar mahasoos hone vaala badlaav laayaa ja saktaa he
 Had the Prime Minister seen these figures after coming to power, not only the DNA of his policies and programs would have changed but the political dialogue of the BJP should also have been transformed
 surveykshan ke anusaar 200 ru
 250 to Rs
 roj par gujara karne vaali adhikansh aabaadi ke liye bank khate, beemaa vaali jandhan yojana lagbhag bemaani he
 Make in India, Digital India or similar programs can affect a maximum of ten percent of the people
 yahi vajah he ki dihadi par jeene vaale 90 fisadi or unamem bhi adhikansh alpashikshit or ashikshit bharat par modi sarkaar ke mishan or skiimon kaa asar najar nahin aayaa he
 The socio-economic reality of the country lies in his hands before Modi's policies wane
 in aankadon kii roshni main ve nitiyon or gavarnence kii nai shuruyaat kar sakate hai, kyonki unhen logon ne nai shuruyaat ke liye hi chunaa he, ateet kii lakiron par nae rang-rogan ke liye nahin

 chunaav purv surveykshan darshata he ki congress party 74-84 siten jeet sakati he, jisane 2014 main keval 44 siten jiti thim

 sanyukt pragatisheel gathbandhan (samprag) ko 115 se 135 siten milane kii sambhaavna jataai gai he

 agar tisare morche ke gathan kii sambhaavna banati he to bhaajapa or congress ke kuch saajhedaar bhi usamen shaamil ho sakate hai

 police ne shanivaar ko yah jaankaree di

 centre sarkaar ne vodaphone se jude transfar prising maamle main bombai hoicourt ke faisle ke khilaaf apil nahin karne kaa faisla kiya he
 The sources gave this information after the meeting of the Union Cabinet
 yah maamla wadaphone kii bhartiya ikai ke sheyaron ko britain kii apni paitruk company ko hastantarit karte samay lagaai gai keemat se judaa he
 The High Court had ruled that Vodafone does not incur a liability of Rs 3200 crore in this case
 ab sarkaar ne nirnay kiya he ki vah vodaphone maamle main bombai hoicourt ke faisle ke khilaaf apil nahin karegi
 The decision not to appeal in the Vodafone case has been taken following the opinion of Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi
 rohtagi ne iskar vibhaag ko salaah di thi ki vah vodaphone maamle main bombai hoicourt ke faisle ko sweekaar kare
 It is worth noting that the High Court, in its order on 10 October 2014, while giving huge relief to the mobile service company Vodafone, said that it is not liable to pay tax of Rs 3200 crore in the matter related to transfer pricing
 iskar vibhaag ne company par aarope lagaaya tha ki usne apni ikai vodaphone ke sheyaron kaa mulya kam rakhaa, jabaki unhen britain main paitruk company ko transfar kiya gaya tha
 The department had demanded additional income tax from the company
 sheyaron kaa yah len-dein vitt varsh 2010 main hua tha
 Vodafone approached the Bombay High Court on 27 January challenging the order of the Income Tax Department
 ---input bhashaa se The Goods and Services Tax (GST) amendment bill, considered to be beneficial for the common citizens and the government, passed in the Rajya Sabha on Wednesday
 upree sadan main kareeb 8 ghante kii lambii charchaa ke baad der shaam bill par voting hui
 203 votes were cast in favor of the amendment bill, while Jayalalithaa's party AIADMK did not participate in voting
 bill ke paas hone ke baad pradhanmantri narendra modi ne twit kar sabhi dalon or unke sadasyon ko dhanyavad kaha
 At the same time, Finance Minister Arun Jaitley celebrated the happiness by cutting the cake after passing the bill
 isse pehle unhone hi sanshodhit bill ko sadan ke patal par rakhaa tha
 He called GST the most important tax reform of the past decade
 jetali ne bataaya ki jiesti se bharat ek samaan market main badal jayega
 He said that the Rajya Sabha had submitted the GST bill to the Select Committee
 zyaadaatar dalon main is bill ko lekar sahmati ban gai he
 He said that this will bring a big change in the country
 jetali ne kaha ki ve sabhi partiyon ke abhaari hai
 Not only this, Jaitley also thanked Congress leader Ghulam Nabi Azad
 i would like to add that GST will also be the best example of cooperative federalism
 Together we will take India to new heights of progress— Narendra Modi (@narendramodi) August 3, 2016 i also thank media, intellectuals, economists and members of civil society for creating an enabling environment for the passage of # gstbill
 — Amit Shah (@amitshah)august 3, 2016I congratulate PM Sh@narendramodiand FM Sh@arunjaitelyfor creating wide consensus on # gstbillthat will benefit all including poor
 - Amit Shah (@amitshah) August 3, 2016 Tamil Nadu CM Jayalalithaa's party AIADMK has decided to propose 6 amendments to the GST bill
 gulam nabi ne kaha- sarkaar kii madad karengecongress netaa gulam nabi aaazaad ne kaha tha ki ve jiesti par sarkaar kii madad karenge
 Azad said that the amendments suggested by his party and leaders have been included in the bill
 isliye ab ve iskaa samarthan karenge
 Chidambaram said- 'welcome' Former Finance Minister p Chidambaram was appearing on behalf of the Congress on the GST bill in the Rajya Sabha
 unhone kaha ki ve is bill kaa swaagat karte hai
 He said that in the last few weeks there has been a change in the attitude of the government regarding the bill
 isliye congress is bill kaa swaagat karti he
 Must read: Who said what on the GST amendment bill from these 20 things? a tax rule will be implemented in the whole country after GST is implemented
 philhal logon ko 30 se 35 pratishat tak tex bharna padataa he
 But with the implementation of GST, people will have to pay only half of it ie 17 to 18 percent tax
 jiesti lagu ho jane se exise tex, sarvice tex, waite, cells tex, antertenment tex or lagjri tex khatm ho jayega
 Expecting the help of Congress after these major changes 1
 rajyon ke bich hone vaale kaarobaar main ek pratishat edishnal tex nahin lagegaa
 2
 rajyon ko agar jiesti se nuksaan hoga to centre sarkaar 5 saal tak 100 pratishat muaavja degi
 This is how the GST Bill will be passed in the Lok Sabha last year
 ab rajyasabha main paas hone ke baad bhi ise kam se kam 15 rajyon kii vidhansabhaon kii manjuuri chahie
 After this approval, the bill will be sent to the President
 raashtrapati ke hastakshar ke baad yah vidheyak kanoon ban jayega
 However, after this, the central government will have to make laws related to GST for the center and the state
 vaajapeyi sarkaar ne rakhi thi jiesti kii neenvgauratlab he ki jiesti kii neenv 16 baras pehle vaajapeyi sarkaar ne daali thi
 The 360 degree rotation is expected to pass in the Rajya Sabha on Wednesday, because 16 years ago the Vajpayee government could not submit if it was in a minority and in 2009, the Manmohan government tried, then the non-congress ruled states protested
 ab centre or zyaadaatar rajyon main bijepi kii bahumat vaali sarkarein hai, to rajyasabha main congress ko saath lene ke liye modi sarkaar apane rukh thode naram kiye
 After which agreement was reached with Congress
 aam aadmi ko jiesti se phaayde kii ummidek desh ek tex kii soch desh main lagu hote hi iskaa phayda har vyakti ko milegaa
 With this, more than 20 indirect taxes will be eliminated and only three types (central, State and Integrated GST) will be taxed
 central jiesti tex centre sarkaar vasuulegi
 The State GST tax will be levied by the State Government, and the Integrated GST will be levied by the Central States, as it will be levied on the trade between the two states
 kuch chijen sasti hongi to kuch mahangi bhijaahir he ye sawaal har jahan main hoga ki jiesti lagu hone se kya sasta or kya mahangaa hoga? restaraan main khaanaa khaanaa, kanjumar durables masalan air condishan, microwave, mashinari saamaan or maal dhulaai sasti hogi to jabaki dibba band food products, chaay, coffee, mobile bill, cradid card kaa bill, jewelri or kapadaa mahangaa ho jayega
 Due to the implementation of GST, it is possible to increase the growth rate, inflation may also increase by two to three years after the implementation of GST
 vaise sarkaar kaa daawa he ki jiesti lagu hone ke baad growth rate main 2% kaa ijapha hoga
 However, the truth is that no government has been reelected in the elections held after the implementation of GST all over the world, because some things become expensive in the initial years, the government has to suffer

 The eunuchs have demanded that a court case should not be heard in the women's court
 is cese ko kisi anya adaalat main transfar kar diya janaa chahie
 a group of 11 eunuchs in Chennai are facing criminal cases of kidnapping a 19-year-old boy and forcibly conducting a sex change operation
 in kinnaron ne ab ek yachika daayar kar maamla kisi anya court main transfar kiye jane kii maang kii he
 These kin accused have stated in their plea that they are neither men nor women, therefore a special court should be set up for them
 2009 main 19 varshiya vinod ko in kinnaron ne kidanap kiya tha or is maamle main tamilnadu ke krime branch criminal investigeshan department (CBCID) ne 11 kinnaron ko giraftaar kiya tha or baad main un par chargeshit lagaai thi
 Now these eunuchs have said in their latest petition that Vinod was a man at the time of the charges against him, so this case should be transferred to another court and there should be trial
 haalanki, iske jawaab main CBCID ne kaha he ki haalanki vinod main mahilaon jaise lakshan dikhte the, lekin vah sex badalane ke liye oparation karaane kaa icchhuk nahin tha
 But the accused was forcibly operated
 is yachika ke saath hi kai enjio jo transgenders ke liye kaam kar rahe hai, alert ho gaye hai
 AJ Hariharan, secretary of the Indian Community Welfare Organization (ICWO), an NGO working for hiv-related issues in transgenders in Chennai, says that transgenders are treated like women in general and i am surprised by this petition
